# Effects 

## List of FX Effects

!!!warning Attention!

Some effects are looped even with false and need to be stopped forcefully!

```lua
GRAPHICS.ANIMPOSTFX_PLAY(effectName, 1, false)
GRAPHICS.ANIMPOSTFX_STOP(effectName)
```
!!!
